Arachne- A 3D Printed Building Facade by Lei Yu</p></div>\n<p>Awards are the icing on your CV, if you know what I mean. So why not take advantage of a new entry date for A’ Design Award and Competition?</p>\n<p>Essentially, the A’ Design Award and Competition is the world’s most inclusive and largest design competition that rewards creatives with highly sought-after prizes and industry insights and feedback. It aims to highlight the best designs, concepts and design-oriented products around the globe each year. The deadline for submission is September 30th, 2018.</p>\n<p>If you’re a designer (of any kind), there is a category in the competition for you. The full list includes 100 different categories such as <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-industrial-design.html\">Good Industrial Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-architecture-design.html\">Good Architecture Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-product-design.html\">Good Product Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-communication-design.html\">Good Communication Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-service-design.html\">Good Service Design </a>and <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-fashion-design.html\">Good Fashion Design</a>. You can find more design categories <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/categories.html\">here</a>.</p>\n<p>Nominate your designs for award consideration <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/registration.php\">here</a>.</p>\n<p><span id=\"more-153318\"></span></p>\n<p>Entries will be judged by an international jury panel of academics, design professionals, and press members using fair evaluation and an extensive methodology.</p>\n<p>The comprehensive A’ Design Award Winners Kit is, of course, one of the main reason many register and compete in the A’ Design Award and Competition. Just some of the benefits this award package includes are: participation in an exhibition at the Museum of Outstanding Design (MOOD), inclusion in an annual hardcover yearbook, publicity by way of tools such as a press release and marketing, inclusion in the World Design Rankings, an invitation to the A’ Design Award Gala-Night in Como, Italy, an award trophy (<a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/trophy-images.html\">check it out</a>), feedback notes from the jury, press release translation into more than 20 languages, the Prime Design Mark, and participation in a extensive PR campaign. However, many say that the feedback from experienced professionals alone is the most valuable prize. This strong jury brings knowledge and insight to each category, evaluating them expertly and providing valuable feedback experience from a panel of from industry leaders, academics and prestigious journalists.</p>\n<p>The deadline for submission is September 30th, 2018. You can learn more about the A’ Design Award and Competition at <a href=\"http://www.designaward.com/\">designaward.com</a>.</p>\n<div id=\"attachment_153324\" style=\"width: 575px\" class=\"wp-caption-text\">Or2 Photochromatic Canopy Structure by Orproject</p></div>\n<p>The A’ Design Award &#38; Competition is one of the largest and leading truly global design competitions. The competition seeks to recognize and award the best designs and well-designed products from around the world. The registration period is now open and you can nominate your design <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/registration.php\">here</a>.</p>\n<p>Are you an artist or designer? If so, there is a category for your work. In fact, there are 100 main categories including Unexpected Design; Interior Space and Exhibition Design; Arts, Crafts and Ready-Made Design; Website and Web Design; Photography and Photo Manipulation Design; Fashion, Apparel and Garment Design; and Sustainable Products, Projects and Green Design. You can browse all of the competition&#8217;s categories <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/design-award-categories.html\">here</a>.</p>\n<p>For competition winners, the A’ Design Award is actually part of an extensive winners’ kit. This winners’ kit includes a certificate and trophy, inclusion in a hard-cover yearbook publication and physical exhibition, invitations to a gala celebration in Italy and much more. Further, winners enjoy benefits such as marketing, consulting, inclusion in World Design Ranking, press release and press kit preparation and distribution and translation of a summary of your project into more than 20 languages. Entries will be judged by an international jury panel of academics, design professionals and press members following a strict and thorough methodology.</p>\n<p>As mentioned earlier, the registration period is now open and the deadline for regular submissions is September 30. Learn more about the A’ Design Awards &#38; Competition and register your project <a href=\"http://www.whatisadesignaward.com/\">here</a>. In the meantime check out some of the past awarded projects and designs.</p>\n<p><span id=\"more-153093\"></span></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_153100\" style=\"width: 575px\" class=\"wp-caption 09:15:06","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 09:15:06","title":"6th Annual Art Bingo: Playing Bingo For Fun, For Art, And For the Community With Local Boston Art Charity","link":"http://beautifuldecay.com/?p=153050","description":"<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-153051 size-full\" src=\"http://beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/12963759_1085464768173399_2148792509528028504_n.jpg\" alt=\"12963759_1085464768173399_2148792509528028504_n\" width=\"565\" height=\"565\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/12963759_1085464768173399_2148792509528028504_n.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/12963759_1085464768173399_2148792509528028504_n-300x300.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /> <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/TheArtConnection/photos/a.204883889564829.59886.195548520498366/1085464768173399/?type=3&#38;theater\">source</a><br />\n<span lang=\"EN-GB\">Do you like the arts? (Spoiler alert: if you are browsing this website, you probably do). Do you believe that more people should have access to art and have the chance appreciate original artwork from their local community? Good. Now, do you like bingo?</span></p>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">If you are wondering what one has to do with the other, then you must have missed last week’s <a href=\"http://www.theartconnection.org/\">Art Bingo event with the Art Connection</a> – a nonprofit program established in 1995 that connects artists and donors to community service organizations through the placement of original artwork. The charity finds homes for art pieces (donated by local artists and collectors) in healing environments, where the artworks serve to enliven the spaces and become points of inspiration that allow their recipients opportunity for reflection, comfort, and hope.</span></p>\n<p><span id=\"more-153050\"></span></p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-153052 size-full\" src=\"http://beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/BD-image-1.jpg\" alt=\"BD image 1\" width=\"565\" height=\"319\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/BD-image-1.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/BD-image-1-300x169.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/BD-image-1-500x282.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /><a href=\"https://pixabay.com/el/bingo-τοκομερίδιο-τυχερός-εισιτήριο-987408/\">source</a></p>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">Recent placements include BEST Corporation, Elder Service Plan of Harbor Health, South End Community Health Center, and Victory Programs. So far the Art Connection has placed over 7,500 original artworks (generously donated by over 450 artists and collectors) in over 400 agencies. The declared and noble mission of Art Connection is to promote access to art in under-served communities – and what better way to achieve that than by coming together to play?</span></p>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">Why bingo, you say? Well, simply because it continues to be an immensely popular game of chance, easy to understand and familiar to everybody – it has even conquered the Internet, which has seen several <a href=\"https://www.sunbingo.co.uk/\">gaming websites hosting online bingo games</a>. Usually, such websites involve extra features that attract players, such as multi-room bingo –where players have the option to launch and play in more than one bingo room at a time– or bingo chat (complete with emoticons) to communicate with fellow players and make the game more social.</span></p>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">Bingo games remain very popular with charities in particular. The rules are simple: the game host draws numbers at random and each player takes care to match them on 5&#215;5 cards, pre-printed in different arrangements. When a row is formed by the random numbers, the player calls out &#8220;Bingo!&#8221; to signal their win and claim the designated prize. In the case of Art Bingo the prize is one of twelve original artworks by local artists – so that every winner can take a piece home and become a proud art collector.</span></p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-153053 size-full\" src=\"http://beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/BD-image-2.jpg\" alt=\"BD image 2\" width=\"565\" height=\"347\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/BD-image-2.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/BD-image-2-300x184.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/BD-image-2-488x300.jpg 488w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p><a href=\"https://pixabay.com/el/bingo-τύχη-παιχνίδι-παίξετε-1044718/\">source</a></p>\n<p><a href=\"http://www.artweekboston.org/event/art-bingo-2017-with-the-art-connection/\">The event formed part of ArtWeek Boston</a>, a biannual creative festival first established in Boston that features a wide range of events and interactive experiences throughout all of Eastern Massachusetts. This was the 6<sup>th</sup> annual Art Bingo organized and, as has become a tradition each year, one of the dozen games played showcases and promotes the work of a talented emerging visual artist from local Boston Arts Academy. Art Bingo also features premium silent auctions, with prizes this year ranging from ticket packages to Boston’s best theaters to gift certificates to dine in award winning local restaurants.</p>\n<p>This year, guests crowded the lobby of the historic Ben Franklin Institute to engage with artwork and mingle with artists before attending the fast-paced games and auctions. The event saw Boston City Councilor Ayanna Pressley return as a bingo caller while VERY <span lang=\"EN-GB\">Gallery’s John Guthrie (also known for his work with Kate Werble Gallery in NYC, Tinku Gallery in Toronto, and Spazio Natta in Italy) has acted as the juror, choosing this year’s art pieces. Selected artists included <a href=\"http://marilynlevinart.com/\">renowned painter and art professor Marilyn Levin</a> and photographer Timothy Wilson, well-known for his unique style that blurs boundaries between painting and photography, focusing more on shape and atmosphere than content or locale.</span></p>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">A highlight of the event was honoring Ellen Rich with the Annual Art BINGO Artist Award – another beloved tradition. Ellen was an original signer on the Art Connection’s bylaws, volunteered in numerous capacities with the program and even donated her own original works throughout the years. Some of her artworks have been placed with nonprofits such as New England Center for Homeless Veterans, Pine Street Inn, St. Francis House, Centro Latino de Chelsea, Inc., and East Boston Neighborhood Health Center. Her collage “Marsden” (acrylic on paper) was selected as one of this year’s twelve works up for grabs.</span></p>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">Having fun for a good cause – one that includes building bridges between artists, those deprived of access to art, and the community as a whole. More charities should draw from this example of how to develop a power combination that truly boosts local engagement with the arts.</span></p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/2017/05/19/6th-annual-art-bingo-playing-bingo-fun-art-community-local-boston-art-charity/\">6th Annual Art Bingo: Playing Bingo For Fun, For Art, And For the Community With Local Boston Art Charity</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com\">Beautiful/Decay</a>.</p>\n","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Fri, 19 Awards &#38; Competition is the world’s largest design competition. Juried by experts in the field, the competition recognizes the best and most exciting work in design from around the world.In addition to the award itself, participating and winning the A’ Design Award means recognition, publicity and as well as a long list of other benefits.</p>\n<p>In addition to the sheer size of the competition and it’s extensive winner’s kit, one thing that particularly sets the A’ Design Awards &#38; Competition apart are the categories. Submissions are accepted in dozens of categories ensuring that your work finds its best fit. This includes categories such as <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-industrial-design.html\">Good Industrial Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-architecture-design.html\">Good Architecture Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-product-design.html\">Good Product Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-communication-design.html\">Good Communication Design</a> , <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-service-design.html\">Good Service Design</a>, and <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-fashion-design.html\">Good Fashion Design</a>. You can find further design categories <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-fashion-design.html\">here</a>.</p>\n<p><span id=\"more-153216\"></span></p>\n<p>As mentioned, the A’ Design Prize is actually a comprehensive kit. This includes perks such as participation in an international exhibition, inclusion in annual hardcover yearbook, a press release, publicity through the Competition’s extensive network, inclusion in the World Design Rankings, an invitation to a gala-night event in Italy for a unique networking opportunity, an award trophy and certificate, translation services for your press release into more than 20 languages, feedback notes from the jurors, a Designer of the Year nomination, sales listing for your winning design and much more.</p>\n<p>Entries to the Competition are judges by an international jury panel of scholars, industry experts and prominent journalists. Unlike many other awards, the A’ Design Awards &#38; Competition follows a strict methodology including, a peer-review process with anonymous voting and evaluation of entries.</p>\n<p>You can learn everything you need to know about the competition at <a href=\"http://www.designaward.com/\">designaward.com</a>. Yuanwei by LIANG HONGNING (Winner 2019)</p></div>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’re a designer (of any kind), and you want to top off your CV this year with incredible recognition, the A’ Design Award and Competition is announcing a new submission day. The A’ Design Award and Competition is the world’s most inclusive and largest design competition that rewards creatives with highly sought-after prizes and industry insights and feedback. It aims to highlight the best designs, concepts and design-oriented products around the globe each year. There’s an early deadline on June 30th, the regular deadline is September 30th, and the late deadline is February 28th, 2020. The winners will be announced on April 15th, 2020. Throughout this post view some of the most recent winners! </span></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_153440\" style=\"width: 575px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-153440\" Zhang (Winner 2019)</p></div>\n<p><span id=\"more-153437\"></span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’re thinking about applying and you’re not sure “you fit the mold”, don’t worry! There is a category in the competition for you. The full list includes 100 different categories such as </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-industrial-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Industrial Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-architecture-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Architecture Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-product-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Product Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-communication-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Communication Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-service-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Service Design </span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">and </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-fashion-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Fashion Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. You can find more design categories </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/categories.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">here</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Nominate your designs for award consideration </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/registration.php\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">here</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Entries will be judged by an international jury panel of academics, design professionals, and press members using fair evaluation and an extensive methodology.</span></p>\n<div id=\"attachment_153448\" style=\"width: 575px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img Water by Lucy Yip (Winner 2019)</p></div>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The comprehensive A’ Design Award Winners Kit is, of course, one of the main reason many register and compete in the A’ Design Award and Competition. Just some of the benefits this award package includes are: participation in an exhibition at the Museum of Outstanding Design (MOOD), inclusion in an annual hardcover yearbook, publicity by way of tools such as a press release and marketing, inclusion in the World Design Rankings, an invitation to the A’ Design Award Gala-Night in Como, Italy, an award trophy (</span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/trophy-images.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">check it out</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">), feedback notes from the jury, press release translation into more than 20 languages, the Prime Design Mark, and participation in a extensive PR campaign. However, many say that the feedback from experienced professionals alone is the most valuable prize. This strong jury brings knowledge and insight to each category, evaluating them expertly and providing valuable feedback experience from a panel of from industry leaders, academics and prestigious journalists.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The late deadline for submission is February 28, 2020. The winners will be released to the public on April 15th, 2020. To see more information about the deadlines go <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/design-award-dates.html\">here</a>.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can learn more about the A’ Design Award and Competition at </span><a href=\"http://www.designaward.com/\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">designaward.com</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 09:15:06","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 09:15:06","title":"10 Cool Logo Designs","link":"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/?p=153415","description":"<p>It doesn’t matter how creative you are as an individual, there are times when ideas just refuse to come to you. In situations like these, what you usually need is some inspiration. So, if you want to create some of the most amazing logo designs, then you can check out the following examples to get your creative juices flowing:</p>\n<ol>\n<li><strong> BadgehuntingClub </strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153416\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/1-565x424.jpg\" alt=\"1\" width=\"565\" height=\"424\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/1-565x424.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/1-300x225.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/1-400x300.jpg 400w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/1.jpg 571w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p>This logo is an excellent example of how you can bring two different design styles together to create a unique effect. As you can see, it combines vintage flare with contemporary pop which makes for a distinct appeal. What’s more interesting is that it’s designed by the well-known designer Allan Peters. In fact, you can see more of his designs in the same format <a href=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/2016/01/15/allan-peters-combines-vintage-flare-with-contemporary-pop-in-his-dynamic-branding-and-logos/\">here</a>.</p>\n<ol start=\"2\">\n<li><strong> Wild Wild Wings<br />\n</strong><strong><br />\n<img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153417\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/2-565x477.jpg\" alt=\"2\" width=\"565\" height=\"477\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/2-565x477.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/2-300x253.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/2-355x300.jpg 355w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/2.jpg 571w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></strong></li>\n<li><strong> BBC (Baker Bar Coffee)</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153418\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/3-565x424.jpg\" alt=\"3\" width=\"565\" height=\"424\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/3-565x424.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/3-300x225.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/3-399x300.jpg 399w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/3.jpg 571w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" />Sometimes, combining two different icons and visual elements can create interesting designs. That’s exactly what’s happened here. The artist Yuri Kartashev took two main elements of the brand i.e. food and drinks and combined their visual representations- spatula (food) and bottles (bar). He also cleverly adorned the unique icon with the highlights of the brand in a circle (Baker, Bar, Coffee).</p>\n<p><span id=\"more-153415\"></span></p>\n<p><strong>Tailor Brands</strong><br />\n<img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153419\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/4-565x283.jpg\" alt=\"4\" width=\"565\" height=\"283\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/4-565x283.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/4-300x150.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/4-500x250.jpg 500w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/4.jpg 570w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p>This logo design is particularly interesting. This is because it belongs to the <a href=\"https://www.tailorbrands.com/\">Tailor Brands</a>platform which itself provides AI-powered logo design services to those who want instant and affordable results. Understandably, the design is beyond impressive on many levels. For starters, the icon is ambiguous which means that some people will see a pencil in it while others will see a heart or diamond or even all of them together, and that’s really the beauty of it. Also, they decided to stick with just one color i.e. reddish pink which not only creates a powerful impact but also maintains brand consistency.</p>\n<ol start=\"5\">\n<li><strong> Movers</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153420\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/5-565x395.jpg\" alt=\"5\" width=\"565\" height=\"395\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/5-565x395.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/5-300x209.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/5-430x300.jpg 430w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/5.jpg 570w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p>Have you ever paid a closer look at the FedEx logo? If you have, then you must have realized that it uses negative space. In fact, it’s one of the best examples to demonstrate the <a href=\"https://www.deluxe.com/sbrc/logo/less-is-more-the-power-of-negative-space-logos\">power of negative space logos</a>. The above logo is another great example to learn this technique. It uses the negative space below the hand which creates an image of ahouse. However, it also shows the action of the brand i.e. “moving” (your home) from one place to another.</p>\n<ol start=\"6\">\n<li><strong> Giant Owl Productions (Animated Logo)</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153421\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/6-565x377.jpg\" alt=\"6\" width=\"565\" height=\"377\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/6-565x377.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/6-184x124.jpg 184w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/6-300x200.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/6-450x300.jpg 450w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/6.jpg 570w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p>With animation, you can grab the attention of the target demographic easily compared to a static image, and this logo proves the point. The key is using movements that aren’t too distracting or over the top. Also, it’s important that the logolooks good even when it’s static as you won’t be able to show the animation everywhere (think about billboards, business cards, etc.).</p>\n<p>Creating an animated logo is actually quite easy. You can find several tutorials online. If you want to learn it professionally, then you can also take the course <a href=\"https://www.udemy.com/living-logos-animation-simple-after-effects/\">here</a>.</p>\n<ol start=\"7\">\n<li><strong> Jenny Ketan Photography</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153422\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/7-565x310.jpg\" alt=\"7\" width=\"565\" height=\"310\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/7-565x310.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/7-300x165.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/7-500x275.jpg 500w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/7.jpg 570w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p>You don’t always need unique icons or visual metaphors to create attractive logos as shown in the example above. If you are able to find a distinct font or type for a brand, then that can get the desired effect without any problem. Remember Coca-Cola? Its iconic logo is known across the world because of the calligraphy that’s particular to the brand.</p>\n<ol start=\"8\">\n<li><strong> SixlocksSecurity</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153423\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/8-565x300.jpg\" alt=\"8\" width=\"565\" height=\"300\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/8-565x300.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/8-300x159.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/8-500x266.jpg 500w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/8.jpg 570w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p>If your brand name has a number, then you can incorporate it in the logo icon. The logo above is a good example, as you can see the “six” from Sixlocksis used in a creative manner in the icon that represents both the nature of the business and the brand name.</p>\n<ol start=\"9\">\n<li><strong> Thirsty Peacock</strong></li>\n</ol>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153424\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/9-565x342.jpg\" alt=\"9\" width=\"565\" height=\"342\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/9.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/9-300x182.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/9-496x300.jpg 496w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153425\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/10-565x354.jpg\" alt=\"10\" width=\"565\" height=\"354\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/10-565x354.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/10-300x188.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/10-479x300.jpg 479w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/03/10.jpg 570w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p>In this age of automation, technology, and machines, a “human touch” can help any piece of art to stand out. So, instead of taking a mechanical approach towards creating a logo design, you can ask a designer to create a hand-drawn logo for you just like the one above. It might cost you a lot more than online logo makers, but the impact will be incredible.</p>\n<p>So, there you have it- some of the most creative logo designs that you can draw inspiration from. http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/08/unnamed1.jpg 1600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p>Lover of nature and photography? There are some good news for you! The Weather Channel and Toyota have come together once again to find the most beautiful, stimulating, and jaw-dropping photographs in their <a href=\"http://www.weather.com/photos/contest\">“It’s Amazing Out There”</a> photos competition. Both amateur and professional photographers are invited to submit their most spectacular images that best depict the wonder, impact, and beauty of Mother Nature.</p>\n<p>You may be asking yourself if pictures of tornadoes, hurricanes or lightning are only applicable for this contest. The answer is “no.” The weather channel recognizes that “weather” is so much more than the forecast or even weather elements, nature alone should do.</p>\n<p>We want YOU to submit works that fall under the categories of nature, adventure and/or the elements. The first prize is a whopping $15,000 with a second prize of $5,000, and third prize of $2,500. Three fan favorites will take home $1,000, $750 and $500.</p>\n<p>Just think about all of the lenses and photo paper you can buy with that kind of dough!</p>\n<p>The deadline for the “It’s Amazing Out There” contest is August 14th at noon ET.  Read the complete rules <a href=\"http://(http://bit.ly/1RQyEnY\">HERE</a> And enter your photograph <a href=\"http://www.weather.com/photos/contest\">HERE</a>.</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" Entries are due by February  28th 2019!</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The A’ Design Award and Competition is the world’s most inclusive and largest design competition that rewards creatives with highly sought-after prizes and industry insights and feedback. Its purpose is to highlight the best designs, concepts and design-oriented products around the globe each year. The prize kit is beyond beneficial to your career as it not only includes cash prizes but incredible opportunities to network and expert advice from experienced design professionals. </span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">If you’re a designer, there is a category in the competition for you. The full list includes 100 different categories such as </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-industrial-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Industrial Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-architecture-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Architecture Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-product-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Product Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-communication-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Communication Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-service-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Service Design </span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">and </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-fashion-design.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Good Fashion Design</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. You can find more design categories </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/categories.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">here</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Nominate your designs for award consideration </span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/registration.php\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">here</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">.</span></p>\n<p><span id=\"more-153397\"></span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Entries will be judged by an international jury panel of academics, design professionals, and press members using fair evaluation and an extensive methodology.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The comprehensive A’ Design Award Winners Kit is, of course, one of the main reason many register and compete in the A’ Design Award and Competition. Just some of the benefits this award package includes are: participation in an exhibition at the Museum of Outstanding Design (MOOD), inclusion in an annual hardcover yearbook, publicity by way of tools such as a press release and marketing, inclusion in the World Design Rankings, an invitation to the A’ Design Award Gala-Night in Como, Italy, an award trophy (</span><a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/trophy-images.html\"><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">check it out</span></a><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">), feedback notes from the jury, press release translation into more than 20 languages, the Prime Design Mark, and participation in a extensive PR campaign. However, many say that the feedback from experienced professionals alone is the most valuable prize. </span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Entries will be judged by an international jury panel of academics, design professionals, and press members using fair evaluation and an extensive methodology.</span> This strong jury brings knowledge and insight to each category, evaluating them expertly and providing valuable feedback experience from a panel of from industry leaders, academics and prestigious journalists.</p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The deadline for submission is F</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">ebruary 28</span><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">. The winners will be released to the public on April 15th, 2019.</span></p>\n<p><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">You can learn more about the A’ Design Award and Competition at </span><a Casal-Data","articleImgCdnMap":{"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/3f8b937210a8e0fcc7d39d717e3edf35a777dd00-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn31@2020_6/2020/08/25/01-15-06-701_b9039819a481deb8.webp","http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/4af4b89840a0b6790cb675f2ab2ed06377312d95-1-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn39@2020_1/2020/08/25/01-15-48-097_bcb0140912d2def1.webp","http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/25a6aa0816f0c23f8fb39579b151376ba1e9b70c-4-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn83@2020_3/2020/08/25/01-15-36-697_c34d155e3540b7a4.webp","http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/9853357b4491d916b6af53e31713b5a7696663e9-3-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn52@2020_2/2020/08/25/01-15-18-747_34e96fa397b89ce2.webp","http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/dbdcd70c1398903aa056f09dfade4aaf45acb21d-2-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn100@2020_5/2020/08/25/01-15-48-949_32777407e8f7aab8.webp","http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/516e2cf675218e3854769674fb4d2b428214aa72-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn92@2020_4/2020/08/25/01-15-18-652_6eb5a4e8fd51d4e7.webp","http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/309426d1a7bf8a64c0a7e674a5c6f4bebd77ee0c-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn43@2020_5/2020/08/25/01-15-43-836_5ffc54ffeaa98c09.webp","http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/ad55e51be80ec61544d413a23ef849d1610f51db-4-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn84@2020_5/2020/08/25/01-15-20-924_d43099719e2741dc.webp","http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/bafc436418b6f7a837c8239c7958de5f8d667f18-2-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn100@2020_6/2020/08/25/01-15-40-142_2c465124d3b18019.webp","http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/d443ef04615f3194ada4999184e98da5e4f400d9-1-t710-565x565.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn92@2020_6/2020/08/25/01-15-20-961_dc45b9ff47c85020.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598318106403},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 09:15:06","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 09:15:06","title":"Are You an Art Lover or an Art Collector?","link":"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/?p=153234","description":"<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">For art traders, buying and selling art has been a more lucrative way of making money than other investments. In fact, many have built a <a href=\"https://www.bloomberg.com/features/2015-michele-maccarone-art-dealer/\">growing and rewarding business</a>.</span></p>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">The first thing that anyone who is interested in buying art needs to decide is which role they want to play; dealer, investor, or collector. Each has its own motivation, trading strategy, and overall objective. The dealer buys what he believes will fetch the highest price in the short-term, the investor what he feels is the right painting at the right time, and the collector, simply what he likes. When it comes to buying, each of these roles comes with its own strict criteria.</span></p>\n<h2><span lang=\"EN-GB\">The Dealer</span></h2>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">The dealer involves himself in buying and selling paintings, as well as in brokering transactions. Like other business owners, he is talking with customers and suppliers on the telephone every day, be it with other dealers, auction rooms, galleries, collectors, or investors. Dealing has increased in popularity, following other home business trends, such as online auction sales and drop shipping. Others prefer a business model that allows them to <a href=\"https://www.ig.com/uk\">trade from home without having to carry stock</a>, such as spread betting. With spread betting, you can gain leverage by benefitting from comparatively small price movement, and gear your portfolio for greater exposure or make your capital go further. While not altogether the same, there are some similarities to that of the art dealer.</span></p>\n<h2><span lang=\"EN-GB\">The Investor</span></h2>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">The investor has a specific outcome in mind when he makes a purchase. He buys strategically, according to his financial plan and strict criteria, conducting extensive research in a bid to minimise risk. His timeframe is typically between five and seven years out. An economy that is performing poorly will recover within this time. Even a painting no longer considered fresh, such as one that has been unsuccessfully shopped around or recently sold at a public auction, will be considered fresh again. He buys what he believes collectors will love, in order to give him a quick sale. He expects a 25 percent return on investment (ROI) but is confident that he can make an even higher return.</span></p>\n<h2><span lang=\"EN-GB\">The Collector</span></h2>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">The collector has <a href=\"https://www.huffingtonpost.com/paul-klein/the-passion-of-an-exempla_b_125649.html\">a passion for art</a>, but buys it at his own leisure, without any strategy to speak of or any consideration for what kind of painting is trending. He buys whatever pleases him at the time, and may only buy once a year. He has no financial objective or exit strategy to speak of. He may even keep a painting his entire life, ultimately leaving it to a museum or his children. Serious collectors typically have a narrow focus on a particular kind of art and become experts in their chosen speciality.</span></p>\n<p><span lang=\"EN-GB\">If you come across a painting that you like, and its condition is good to excellent; it&#8217;s fairly priced, within your price range, and you’ve done your homework, then buy it. You can simply enjoy it for its aesthetic qualities, or benefit from its profit appreciation for as long as you wish.</span></p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/2018/04/12/art-lover-art-collector/\">Are You an Art Lover or an Art Collector?</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com\">Beautiful/Decay</a>.</p>\n","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Thu, 12 Apr 2018 15:22:14 +0000","feedId":11118,"bgimg":"","linkMd5":"dfdf698223057af5c869ea49584c56e7","bgimgJsdelivr":"","metaImg":"","author":"Russ Crest","publishedOrCreatedDate":1598318106405},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 09:15:06","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 09:15:06","title":"A’ Design Awards & Competition – Last Call for Entries","link":"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/?p=153201","description":"<div id=\"attachment_153211\" style=\"width: 575px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-153211\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/The-Broccoli-Chair-by-Jie-Luo-565x565.jpg\" alt=\"The Broccoli Chair by Jie Luo\" width=\"565\" height=\"565\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/The-Broccoli-Chair-by-Jie-Luo.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/The-Broccoli-Chair-by-Jie-Luo-300x300.jpg 300w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /><p class=\"wp-caption-text\">The Broccoli Chair by Jie Luo</p></div>\n<div id=\"attachment_153208\" style=\"width: 575px\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-153208\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/02/ResoNet-Pavilion-Sinan-Mansions-Pavilion-by-William-Chen-Creative-Prototyping-Unit-565x565.jpg\" alt=\"ResoNet Pavilion - It aims to highlight the best designs, concepts and design-oriented products around the globe each year.</p>\n<p>In addition to the extensive prize package, the A’ Design Award and Competition also serves as an independent and expert appraisal for design by providing valuable feedback and experience from a panel of from industry leaders, academics and prestigious journalists.</p>\n<p><span id=\"more-153201\"></span></p>\n<p>If you design, there is a category in the competition for you. Indeed, the full list includes 100 different categories including <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-industrial-design.html\">Good Industrial Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-architecture-design.html\">Good Architecture Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-product-design.html\">Good Product Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-communication-design.html\">Good Communication Design</a>, <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-service-design.html\">Good Service Design</a> and <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/good-fashion-design.html\">Good Fashion Design</a>. You can find more design categories <a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/categories.html\">here</a>.</p>\n<p>The comprehensive A’ Design Award Winners Kit, of course, is the main reason many register and compete in the A’ Design Award and Competition. Just some of the benefits this award package includes are participation in an exhibition at the Museum of Outstanding Design (MOOD), inclusion in an annual hardcover yearbook, publicity by way of tools such as a press release and marketing, inclusion in the World Design Rankings, an invitation to the A’ Design Award Gala-Night in Como, Italy, an award trophy (<a href=\"https://competition.adesignaward.com/trophy-images.html\">check it out</a>), feedback notes from the jury, press release translation into more than 20 languages, the Prime Design Mark, and participation in a extensive PR campaign.</p>\n<p>Entries will be judged by an international jury panel of academics, design professionals and press members using fair evaluation and an extensive methodology. This strong jury brings knowledge and insight to each category, evaluating them expertly and providing valuable feedback.</p>\n<p>The deadline for submission is February 28, 2018 and results will be publicly announced on April 15, 2018 (including here, on Beautiful/Decay). You can learn more about the A’ Design Award and Competition at <a href=\"http://www.designaward.com/\">designaward.com</a>.</p>\n<p>Nominate your designs for award consideration <a 09:15:06","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 09:15:06","title":"Street Artists That Make Our World a More Exciting Place","link":"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/?p=153173","description":"<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153184\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-title-7-565x377.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-title-7\" width=\"565\" height=\"377\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-title-7.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-title-7-184x124.jpg 184w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-title-7-300x200.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-title-7-450x300.jpg 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" />It’s safe to say that the art of graffiti, the once loathed medium that was reserved uniquely to the outlaws and high-art mavericks (see: Basquiat), has changed pretty much entirely. With no need to sneak around trash cans and lurk in fog-filled passageways (well &#8211; mostly), most <em>graffeteros</em> these days are highly regarded contemporary artists, while the occasional fling with the other side of the law has turned into a charming postmodern adrenaline hunt.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.canvasdiscount.com/\"><strong>CanvasDiscount.com</strong></a><strong> invites you to a street art gallery where paintings can emerge on a gritty channel side, and every street corner can be instantly changed into a genuine exhibit space!</strong></p>\n<p><span id=\"more-153173\"></span></p>\n<p><strong> <img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153174\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-1-565x377.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-1\" width=\"565\" height=\"377\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-1.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-1-184x124.jpg 184w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-1-300x200.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-1-450x300.jpg 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></strong></p>\n<p>Solidarity</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://travelholic.co/worlds-best-street-art/\"><strong>Source<br />\n</strong></a><em>Vulpes Vulpes </em>stands for red fox in Latin. The artist conceived this illegal piece with the help of the local residents who, apparently, lied about the artist’s whereabouts. A rather simple, biting (no pun intended) representation of the man’s complex political views, it depicts a pack of foxes either devouring a single piece in equal parts or uniting their noses in the same manner musketeers used to cross their rapiers. <em>Vulpes Vulpes</em> is a self-confessed anarchist with unconditional love for foxes. An artist who likes to linger on the edge of the law, <em>Vulpes</em> is producing both legally commissioned artworks and something we’d like to call urban Easter eggs. The latter is usually the artist’s comment on the sociopolitical state of affairs. This particular piece is <em>Vulpes</em>’ take on the issues of economic recession.</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>What Goes in Must Come Out</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153175\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-2-565x330.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-2\" width=\"565\" height=\"330\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-2.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-2-300x175.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-2-500x292.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong>source<br />\n</strong></a>When two street artists come together for a collaborative piece, the results, predictably so, are usually really awesome. This “wall art” jumps on the trend and, just like so many other graffiti outlets these days, is playing around with the concept of dimensionality. Created as a part of the SCOPE Art Show (an annual fair taking place in New York, Miami, and Basel), its authorship is shared between Know Hope and Aakash Nihalani. As you can clearly see, both complement each other’s artistry incredibly well, creating a piece that stuns with its simplicity and the clever use of what little additional details there can be.</p>\n<p>Pratt Style</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153176\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-3-565x486.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-3\" width=\"565\" height=\"486\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-3.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-3-300x258.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-3-349x300.jpg 349w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></strong></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong>source<br />\n</strong></a>Now, Pratt Institute is known for its progressive approach towards the arts and humanities, yet hardly anyone would think of its graduates as the most likely street art prodigies, dodging police in the maze of the urban jungle during the nights and scribbling on paper in the wee hours of the morning. However, with the likes of <em>Leon Reid IV </em>and <em>Cake</em>, it’s safe to say that the prestigious institution has indeed produced some of the most renowned contemporary street artists working today. This piece, however, is created by <em>Willow</em>. Using academic knowledge to conjure surrealist imagery on the local walls? Why not?</p>\n<p>The Reflection</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153177\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-4-565x377.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-4\" width=\"565\" height=\"377\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-4.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-4-184x124.jpg 184w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-4-300x200.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-4-450x300.jpg 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong>source</strong></a><br />\nBorondo’s ability to pick seemingly random places that only add to the effect once the artwork is finished is remarkable on its own merit. If you’re not familiar with Dali’s painting or have no clue as to what the myth’s actually about, the long story short version goes as follows. A handsome thespian hunter that went by the name of Narcissus had a thing for his own reflection. Unable to grasp its beauty, Narcissus gave in and pretty much succumbed to his death due to his own prettiness. Borondo’s choice of location all of a sudden makes that much more sense&#8230;. Just imagine encountering this with no pretext!</p>\n<p>Graphic Detail</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153178\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-5-565x377.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-5\" width=\"565\" height=\"377\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-5.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-5-184x124.jpg 184w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-5-300x200.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-5-450x300.jpg 450w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" />source<br />\n</strong></a>No, this wall is by no means graphic in the Internet sense of the word. Instead, it’s a genuine, large-scale monochromatic outing by the Italian artist known as 2501 (by now, it’s clear that street artists pick their public names with an ingenuity that vastly surpasses their pop music counterparts). Exploiting both abandoned slums somewhere in the outskirts and globally revered art galleries, 2501 twists and bends his lines to conjure compelling sceneries that are juxtaposed with urban and suburban environments to a surprisingly marvelous effect. Peculiarly, it really seems that the geography affects the signature. Just take a look at this and the last entry!</p>\n<p>Bogotá’s Treasure</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153183\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-11-565x342.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-11\" width=\"565\" height=\"342\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-11.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-11-300x182.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-11-496x300.jpg 496w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong>source</strong></a></p>\n<p>It may come to you as a surprise, but when it comes down to distinct, decades-perfected street art cultures, Bogotá takes the cake as a place where this particular medium has flourished like no other. Here, they’re called “Graffeteros,” and instead of being viewed as some sort of savages with illegal habits, they’re actually really embraced by the locals who encourage the group to embellish the facades of their houses and window shutters. Bastardilla, the author of the respective piece, is said to be a member of the Bogotá’s graffiti culture&#8217;s dream team – Animal Power Crew. We may never know, but her solo output is equally fascinating and distinctively Southern American in its richness and tribal undertones.</p>\n<p>Moneyless</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153179\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-7-565x376.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-7\" width=\"565\" height=\"376\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-7.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-7-300x200.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-7-451x300.jpg 451w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" /></strong></a></p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong>source</strong></a></p>\n<p>And, here’s yet another talent in the long line of Italian graffiti artists. With that said, Moneyless (Teo Pirisi) might as well be the most interesting and off-beat character of them all. Utilising the geometrical specifics of the space around him, Moneyless uses fishing line and hooks to create something that’s totally outside the threshold of the traditional street art with simple, geometric formations that present the Platonic viewpoint of geometry being the core attribute of nature. Very minimalistic with an aura of mystery that characterizes all good fine art creations, Moneyless shows us what exactly happens when austerity is used the right way!</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>&#160;</p>\n<p>Contemporary Classic</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153180\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-8-565x353.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-8\" width=\"565\" height=\"353\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-8.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-8-300x187.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-8-480x300.jpg 480w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" />source</strong></a></p>\n<p>This man needs no introduction. Banksy is pretty much the superstar of street art culture and probably the most well-known graffiti practitioner working today. Mostly appearing out of the blue only to disappear under equally mysterious conditions, Banksy adorns the walls of his native Britain (though not limited to) with painfully spot-on statements dwelling upon pop culture phenomena and national/international sociopolitical affairs. Excellently executed both form and content-wise, Banksy playfully challenges law enforcement and civilians to reflect on the issues we would usually prefer to push aside.</p>\n<p>50 Cakes of Gay</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153181\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-9-565x269.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-9\" width=\"565\" height=\"269\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-9.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-9-300x143.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-9-500x238.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" />source</strong></a></p>\n<p>Massive, explosively colorful, and funny, the art of Kashnik is instantly recognizable and cannot be mistaken for somebody else’s. Referring to herself not only as a street artist but a full-fledged street activist, Kashnik paints large-scale murals often featuring a mustached gentleman with two pairs of eyes and often in somewhat kinky situations. However, there’s very little mystique as to why it is so. She is an active combatant for human rights issues with a particular focus on same-sex relationships. With the trademark impressive scope (the astonishing <em>50 Cakes of Gay</em> is still a far cry from being her biggest) and vivid hues, Kashnik juxtaposes shamans, aliens, and gangsters to create a trippy and memorable street art extravaganza.</p>\n<p>Ozmo’s Odyssey</p>\n<p><a href=\"http://trendvisions.lancia.it/en/article/outside-the-box-interview-with-street-artist-aakash-nihalani/fluoparty\"><strong><img class=\"aligncenter size-large wp-image-153182\" src=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-10-565x305.jpg\" alt=\"10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-10\" width=\"565\" height=\"305\" srcset=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-10.jpg 565w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-10-300x162.jpg 300w, http://www.beautifuldecay.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/10-graffiti-artists-that-make-our-world-a-better-place-10-500x270.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 565px) 100vw, 565px\" />source</strong></a></p>\n<p>Wrapping up with what is possibly the most eclectic entry on the list, we have the Italy-based Ozmo. Although his creative output mainly focuses on exercises in portraiture, Ozmo’s oeuvre really has bits and pieces of everything. Producing sharp and edgy social commentary in the vein of Banksy as well as utilizing sheer scale in the same manner the previous entry does, Ozmo is also known for his monochromatic pieces, a technique that seems to be so popular amongst his Italian peers. Blending together technical prowess with a tongue-in-cheek humor and an in-depth knowledge of the history of art, the artist is no stranger to both streets and galleries. Here, you can see the Holy Mother going through some sort of <em>Fallout</em> head wrap glitch thing.</p>\n<p><strong>Explored and compiled by photo printing experts from </strong><a href=\"https://www.canvasdiscount.com/\"><strong>Canvasdiscount.com</strong></a><strong>, &#8211; one of the biggest and best-rated manufacturers and distributors of personalized photo wall decor and lifestyle accessories in the U.S.</strong></p>\n<p>The post <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com/2018/01/28/street-artists-make-world-exciting-place/\">Street Artists That Make Our World a More Exciting Place</a> appeared first on <a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"http://www.beautifuldecay.com\">Beautiful/Decay</a>.</p>\n","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Sun, 28 Jan 2018 19:10:42
